	enum CLB_MODE {
		FGM,
		FG,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_I2 {
		B,
		QX,
		QY,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_I3 {
		C,
		QX,
		QY,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_I4 {
		D,
		E,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_D {
		DI,
		F,
		G,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_X {
		F,
		QX,
	}

	enum CLB_MUX_Y {
		G,
		QY,
	}

	enum FF_MODE {
		FF,
		LATCH,
	}

	enum IO_MUX_O {
		O,
		OQ,
	}

	enum IO_SLEW {
		SLOW,
		FAST,
	}

	enum OSC_MODE {
		DISABLE,
		ENABLE,
		DIV2,
	}

	enum READBACK_MODE {
		COMMAND,
		ONCE,
		DISABLE,
	}

	enum STARTUP_SEQ {
		BEFORE,
		AFTER,
	}

	enum IO_INPUT_MODE {
		TTL,
		CMOS,
	}

	bel_class CLB {
		input A;
		input B;
		input C;
		input D;
		input E;
		input DI;
		input EC;
		input RD;
		input K;
		output X;
		output Y;
		attribute F: bitvec[16];
		attribute G: bitvec[16];
		attribute MODE: CLB_MODE;
		attribute MUX_F2: CLB_MUX_I2;
		attribute MUX_G2: CLB_MUX_I2;
		attribute MUX_F3: CLB_MUX_I3;
		attribute MUX_G3: CLB_MUX_I3;
		attribute MUX_F4: CLB_MUX_I4;
		attribute MUX_G4: CLB_MUX_I4;
		attribute MUX_DX: CLB_MUX_D;
		attribute MUX_DY: CLB_MUX_D;
		attribute MUX_X: CLB_MUX_X;
		attribute MUX_Y: CLB_MUX_Y;
		attribute EC_ENABLE: bool;
		attribute RD_ENABLE: bool;
		attribute READBACK_QX: bitvec[1];
		attribute READBACK_QY: bitvec[1];
	}

	bel_class TBUF {
		input I;
		input T;
		bidir O;
	}

	bel_class PULLUP {
		bidir O;
		attribute ENABLE: bool;
	}

	bel_class IO {
		input O;
		input T;
		input IK;
		input OK;
		output I;
		output Q;
		pad PAD: inout
		attribute IFF_MODE: FF_MODE;
		attribute MUX_O: IO_MUX_O;
		attribute SLEW: IO_SLEW;
		attribute READBACK_I: bitvec[1];
		attribute READBACK_IFF: bitvec[1];
		attribute OSC_PULLUP: bool;
	}

	bel_class OSC {
		output O;
		attribute MODE: OSC_MODE;
	}

	bel_class CLKIOB {
		output I;
	}

	bel_class MISC_SW {
		pad M0: input
		pad M1: inout
		attribute READBACK_MODE: READBACK_MODE;
	}

	bel_class MISC_SE {
		pad PROG_B: input
		pad DONE: inout
		attribute TLC: bool;
		attribute DONE_PULLUP: bool;
		attribute REPROGRAM_ENABLE: bitvec[7];
		attribute DONETIME: STARTUP_SEQ;
		attribute RESETTIME: STARTUP_SEQ;
		attribute SLOWOSC_HALT: bool;
	}

	bel_class MISC_NW {
		pad PWRDWN_B: input
		attribute IO_INPUT_MODE: IO_INPUT_MODE;
	}

	bel_class MISC_NE {
		pad CCLK: inout
		attribute TAC: bool;
		attribute POR: bool;
	}

	bel_class MISC_E {
		attribute TLC: bool;
	}

	tile_slot MAIN {
		bel_slot INT: routing;
		bel_slot CLB: CLB;
		bel_slot TBUF[0]: TBUF;
		bel_slot TBUF[1]: TBUF;
		bel_slot TBUF_E[0]: TBUF;
		bel_slot TBUF_E[1]: TBUF;
		bel_slot PULLUP_TBUF[0]: PULLUP;
		bel_slot PULLUP_TBUF[1]: PULLUP;
		bel_slot IO_W[0]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_W[1]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_E[0]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_E[1]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_S[0]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_S[1]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_N[0]: IO;
		bel_slot IO_N[1]: IO;
		bel_slot CLKIOB: CLKIOB;
		bel_slot BUFG: routing;
		bel_slot OSC: OSC;
		bel_slot MISC_SW: MISC_SW;
		bel_slot MISC_SE: MISC_SE;
		bel_slot MISC_NW: MISC_NW;
		bel_slot MISC_NE: MISC_NE;

		tile_class CLB0 {
			cell CELL;
			cell E;
			cell S;
			cell N;
			bitrect MAIN: Vertical (rev 22, rev 8);
			bitrect MAIN_N: Vertical (rev 22, rev 8);

			switchbox INT {
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_A @[MAIN[14][2], MAIN[16][2], MAIN[15][2], MAIN[14][3]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_H[0] = 0b0011,
					CELL.SINGLE_H[2] = 0b1101,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = 0b0110,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = 0b1111,
					CELL.LONG_H[1] = 0b0001,
					CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_S = 0b0100,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_B @[MAIN[19][2], MAIN[17][2], MAIN[20][3], MAIN[17][3], MAIN[18][2]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_H[0] = 0b00011,
					CELL.SINGLE_H[1] = 0b11111,
					CELL.SINGLE_H[3] = 0b00101,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = 0b01111,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = 0b10101,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[4] = 0b10011,
					CELL.LONG_V[0] = 0b00110,
					CELL.OUT_CLB_X_E = 0b10110,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_C @[MAIN[4][2], MAIN[6][3], MAIN[7][2], MAIN[6][2], MAIN[5][2]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[1] = 0b11111,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = 0b00111,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[4] = 0b01011,
					CELL.LONG_V[1] = 0b01001,
					CELL.OUT_CLB_X_W = 0b01100,
					S.SINGLE_H[0] = 0b00101,
					S.SINGLE_H[2] = 0b01110,
					S.SINGLE_H[4] = 0b11101,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_D @[MAIN[0][2], MAIN[1][3], MAIN[0][3], MAIN[1][2]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[1] = 0b0011,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = 0b0101,
					CELL.LONG_H[0] = 0b0100,
					S.SINGLE_H[1] = 0b1111,
					S.SINGLE_H[3] = 0b1110,
					S.OUT_CLB_Y = 0b0010,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_E @[MAIN[21][2], MAIN[20][2]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = 0b01,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[4] = 0b11,
					CELL.LONG_V[1] = 0b00,
					S.SINGLE_H[0] = 0b10,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_DI @[MAIN[7][4], MAIN[10][4], MAIN[11][4], MAIN[7][3]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_H[4] = 0b0011,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = 0b0101,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = 0b1111,
					N.LONG_H[0] = 0b0110,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_EC @[MAIN[14][4], MAIN[15][5], MAIN[15][4], MAIN[15][3]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_H[1] = 0b0011,
					CELL.SINGLE_H[4] = 0b0101,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = 0b1111,
					CELL.LONG_V[0] = 0b0110,
					CELL.LONG_V[1] = 0b1101,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_RD @[MAIN[3][2], MAIN[2][2]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = 0b01,
					CELL.LONG_V[0] = 0b10,
					S.SINGLE_H[2] = 0b11,
					S.LONG_H[1] = 0b00,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_CLB_K @[MAIN[12][4], MAIN[13][4], MAIN[16][5], MAIN[16][4]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[1] = 0b0011,
					CELL.GCLK_V = 0b0101,
					CELL.ACLK_V = 0b0110,
					S.SINGLE_H[3] = 0b1111,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_TBUF_I[0] @[MAIN[8][5]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = 0b1,
					CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_E = 0b0,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_TBUF_I[1] @[MAIN[18][5]] {
					CELL.SINGLE_V[1] = 0b1,
					CELL.OUT_CLB_X_E = 0b0,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_TBUF_T[0] @[MAIN[13][5], MAIN[10][5]] {
					CELL.TIE_0 = 0b01,
					CELL.TIE_1 = 0b11,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = 0b00,
					CELL.LONG_V[0] = 0b10,
				}
				mux CELL.IMUX_TBUF_T[1] @[MAIN[17][5], MAIN[20][5]] {
					CELL.TIE_0 = 0b01,
					CELL.TIE_1 = 0b11,
					CELL.SINGLE_V[4] = 0b10,
					CELL.LONG_V[0] = 0b00,
				}
				progbuf CELL.SINGLE_H[4] = CELL.SINGLE_H_STUB[4] @!MAIN[0][4];
				progbuf CELL.SINGLE_H_STUB[4] = CELL.SINGLE_H[4] @!MAIN[1][4];
				progbuf CELL.SINGLE_V_S[0] = CELL.SINGLE_V_S_STUB[0] @!MAIN_N[20][4];
				progbuf CELL.SINGLE_V_S_STUB[0] = CELL.SINGLE_V_S[0] @!MAIN_N[19][4];
				progbuf CELL.LONG_V[0] = CELL.SINGLE_H[1] @!MAIN[13][3];
				progbuf CELL.LONG_V[1] = CELL.SINGLE_H[2] @!MAIN[8][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_H[0] = CELL.OUT_CLB_X_ES @!MAIN[3][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_H[1] = CELL.LONG_V[0] @!MAIN[14][5];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_H[2] = CELL.LONG_V[1] @!MAIN[9][5];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_H[3] = CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_E @!MAIN[3][4];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_H[4] = CELL.OUT_CLB_X_ES @!MAIN[2][4];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = CELL.LONG_H[1] @!MAIN[21][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[0] = CELL.OUT_CLB_X_E @!MAIN[21][4];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[1] = CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_E @!MAIN[18][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = CELL.LONG_H[0] @!MAIN[11][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[2] = CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_E @!MAIN[9][3];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[3] = CELL.OUT_CLB_X_E @!MAIN[5][4];
				pass CELL.SINGLE_V[4] = CELL.OUT_CLB_Y_E @!MAIN[4][4];
				bipass CELL.SINGLE_H[0] = CELL.SINGLE_H_E[0] @!MAIN[19][6];

			// wire CELL.OUT_IO_N_Q[1]             IO_N[1].Q
		}
	}

	tile_slot LLH {
		bel_slot LLH: routing;

		tile_class LLH_S {
			cell W;
			cell E;
			bitrect MAIN: Vertical (rev 22, rev 13);

			switchbox LLH {
				bipass W.LONG_IO_S[0] = E.LONG_IO_S[0] @MAIN[16][1];
			}
		}

		tile_class LLH_N {
			cell W;
			cell E;
			bitrect MAIN: Vertical (rev 22, rev 10);

			switchbox LLH {
				bipass W.LONG_IO_N[0] = E.LONG_IO_N[0] @MAIN[16][8];
			}
		}
	}

	tile_slot LLV {

		tile_class LLV_W {

		}
	}

	tile_slot MISC_E {
		bel_slot MISC_E: MISC_E;

		tile_class MISC_E {
			bitrect MAIN: Vertical (rev 36, rev 8);

			bel MISC_E {
				attribute TLC @!MAIN[0][0];
			}
		}
	}

	connector_slot W {
		opposite E;

		connector_class PASS_W {
			pass SINGLE_H_E[0] = SINGLE_H[0];

			pass SINGLE_H_E[2] = SINGLE_H[2];

		}
	}
